--- Commit Message ---
LU-18618 ofd: handle filter_fid properly on server

The object's filter_fid could be changed via out_xattr_set(), then the
ofd_object::ofo_ff is out of date, the old ofo_ff layout version could
be a bigger value than that of the merged file, so write/punch upon
this OFD object could be rejected as it prohibit operation with
smaller layout version than that on the disk.

Test-Parameters: testlist=sanity-flr env=ONLY=70a,ONLY_REPEAT=250
Test-Parameters: testlist=sanity-flr env=ONLY=200,ONLY_REPEAT=50

(1 comment)

> Patch Set 22:
> 
> if we don't propagate layout version from MDS to OST, then client has to send something to OST urgently?

--- Message (Alex Zhuravlev, 2025-01-22 06:30:15.000000000) ---
Patch Set 22:

say, we've got two clients, one initiated a layout change, but don't propagate new layout version for a reason (network problem, internal delay, etc). another client got disconnected/evicted from MDS at the same time so can't notice layout change via MDS, but keeps sending RPCs to OST with the old layout version. IMO this is not good.
I understand the old model where MDS holds an layout lock until OSTs get a new version, but not quite understand how we can rely on an unreliable client.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2025-01-22 06:47:50.000000000) ---
Patch Set 23:

I thought this is only *adding* the ability for the client to increase the layout version, but MDS updates are still done?  That would be more robust, so either the MDS or any client with the new layout can update the OST.

If the new MDS is not still updating the layout version, this would break during interop (e.g. old client == no update, new MDS == no update => no layout version update at all).
